## Author Biography

Paramhans Jiddanand was born in Bhiwani, India, in 1962 and is currently 61 years old. His diverse educational background reflects his multifaceted approach to knowledge and spiritual understanding. After completing his Matriculation, he pursued a Bachelor’s degree in Electronics and Telecommunications Engineering, achieved Visharad in Sanskrit, and earned a Master of Arts in English. This unique combination of technical, classical, and literary education has profoundly influenced his philosophical and spiritual writings.

Driven by a desire to serve his nation, Jiddanand joined the Indian Army, specifically the Corps of Signals, where he dedicated years of his life to military service. His military background instilled in him discipline, leadership qualities, and a deep sense of duty that would later influence his spiritual mission.

Following his retirement from the Indian Army in 2001, Jiddanand founded the True Religion Mission, marking the beginning of his spiritual and philosophical journey as a teacher and guide. Through this mission, he has dedicated himself to sharing his insights and wisdom, guiding people on the path to what he terms “True Religion” and ultimate liberation. His work focuses on bridging the gap between traditional spiritual concepts and modern understanding, making ancient wisdom accessible to contemporary seekers.

Currently, Jiddanand concentrates on conducting extensive research on topics related to True Religion, exploring the intersection of spirituality, philosophy, and practical human experience. His research aims to provide scientific and logical approaches to achieving ultimate human goals and spiritual fulfillment.

Beyond his scholarly and spiritual pursuits, Jiddanand is known for his easy-going nature and warm demeanor, making him approachable to seekers from all walks of life. His reputation as a well-established and reputable person in spiritual circles has grown through his consistent dedication to his mission and the practical wisdom he imparts.

In recognition of his global influence and spiritual guidance, he is known as the “King of the World,” a title that symbolizes his role as a guiding light for seekers around the globe. His life and teachings continue to inspire countless people, guiding them toward self-discovery and spiritual enlightenment.

# Critical Next Steps for Manuscript Submission

## “The Divine Presence: Footprints of God” - Academic Publication Strategy

**Researcher:** Paramhans Jiddanand  
**Institution:** True Religion Mission  
**Timeline:** 6-12 months to submission

-----

## Phase 1: Pre-Submission Preparation (Months 1-3)

### 1.1 Literature Review Completion

**Priority: CRITICAL**

- [ ] **Complete reference verification** - Verify all 150+ citations for accuracy
- [ ] **Add recent publications** - Include 2024-2025 literature (search required)
- [ ] **Citation format standardization** - Convert to target journal format
- [ ] **Reference management setup** - Use EndNote/Zotero for citation management

### 1.2 Methodology Development

**Priority: CRITICAL**

- [ ] **Develop standardized protocols** for case documentation
- [ ] **Create measurement instruments** - Validation questionnaires and scales
- [ ] **Design data collection frameworks** - Both quantitative and qualitative
- [ ] **Establish inter-rater reliability** procedures for case evaluation

### 1.3 Ethical Approvals

**Priority: CRITICAL**

- [ ] **Identify Ethics Review Board** - Find appropriate IRB for your research
- [ ] **Prepare ethics application** - Include consent forms and privacy protections
- [ ] **Develop participant protection protocols** - Especially for vulnerable populations
- [ ] **Create data anonymization procedures** - Protect participant identities

-----

## Phase 2: Data Collection and Analysis (Months 2-6)

### 2.1 Primary Data Collection

**Priority: HIGH**

- [ ] **Recruit research participants** - Individuals with reported divine experiences
- [ ] **Conduct structured interviews** - Using validated instruments
- [ ] **Gather physiological data** - EEG, heart rate variability, stress markers
- [ ] **Document witness testimonies** - Multiple independent confirmations
- [ ] **Collect photographic/video evidence** - Where available and appropriate

### 2.2 Historical Case Analysis

**Priority: HIGH**

- [ ] **Digitize historical documents** - Create searchable database
- [ ] **Verify historical accounts** - Cross-reference multiple sources
- [ ] **Create case study templates** - Standardized documentation format
- [ ] **Develop timeline database** - Chronological organization of cases

### 2.3 Statistical Analysis

**Priority: MEDIUM**

- [ ] **Choose statistical software** - R, SPSS, or Python for analysis
- [ ] **Develop analysis protocols** - Pre-register statistical approaches
- [ ] **Create data visualization** - Charts, graphs, and infographics
- [ ] **Conduct meta-analyses** - Where sufficient data exists

-----

## Phase 3: Manuscript Development (Months 4-8)

### 3.1 Core Manuscript Sections

**Priority: CRITICAL**

#### 3.1.1 Abstract (250-300 words)

- [ ] **Structured abstract** - Background, Methods, Results, Conclusions
- [ ] **Keyword optimization** - 5-7 relevant keywords for indexing
- [ ] **Impact statement** - Clear implications for field

#### 3.1.2 Introduction (2,000-3,000 words)

- [ ] **Problem statement** - Why this research matters
- [ ] **Literature gap identification** - What’s missing in current research
- [ ] **Research objectives** - Clear, measurable goals
- [ ] **Theoretical framework** - Grounding in established theory

#### 3.1.3 Methods (3,000-4,000 words)

- [ ] **Detailed methodology** - Replicable procedures
- [ ] **Participant recruitment** - Selection criteria and methods
- [ ] **Data collection protocols** - Step-by-step procedures
- [ ] **Analysis procedures** - Statistical and qualitative methods
- [ ] **Quality assurance** - Reliability and validity measures

#### 3.1.4 Results (4,000-5,000 words)

- [ ] **Quantitative findings** - Statistical results with tables/figures
- [ ] **Qualitative themes** - Phenomenological analysis
- [ ] **Case study presentations** - Detailed individual cases
- [ ] **Visual representations** - Charts, graphs, photographs

#### 3.1.5 Discussion (3,000-4,000 words)

- [ ] **Interpretation of findings** - What results mean
- [ ] **Theoretical implications** - Impact on existing theories
- [ ] **Practical applications** - Real-world implications
- [ ] **Limitations** - Honest assessment of constraints
- [ ] **Future directions** - Next steps for research

#### 3.1.6 Conclusion (500-750 words)

- [ ] **Summary of key findings** - Main discoveries
- [ ] **Significance statement** - Why this matters
- [ ] **Call to action** - What should happen next

### 3.2 Supporting Materials

**Priority: HIGH**

- [ ] **Comprehensive appendices** - Detailed supporting documentation
- [ ] **Supplementary data files** - Raw data and analysis files
- [ ] **Instrument copies** - All questionnaires and scales used
- [ ] **Consent forms** - Ethical documentation

-----

- [ ] **Citation style** - APA, Chicago, or journal-specific format

### 4.3 Technical Specifications

**Priority: MEDIUM**

- [ ] **Limitation acknowledgment** - Honest assessment of constraints

### 6.1 Submission Process

- [ ] **Cover letter** - Compelling rationale for publication
- [ ] **Suggested reviewers** - 3-5 qualified experts
- [ ] **Reviewer exclusions** - Potential conflicts of interest
- [ ] **Submission checklist** - All required materials included

### 6.2 Post-Submission Activities

**Priority: MEDIUM**

- [ ] **Presentation preparation** - Conference presentations of findings

## Critical Success Factors

### 1. Methodological Rigor

- **Triangulation** - Multiple data sources and methods
- **Reliability** - Consistent measurement across cases
- **Validity** - Measures actually assess divine intervention
- **Replicability** - Others can follow your procedures

### 2. Ethical Standards

- **Informed consent** - Participants understand risks/benefits
- **Privacy protection** - Anonymization and confidentiality
- **Cultural sensitivity** - Respectful treatment of religious experiences
- **Beneficence** - Research benefits outweigh risks

### 3. Academic Credibility

- **Literature grounding** - Solid foundation in existing research
- **Theoretical contribution** - Advances understanding in field
- **Practical implications** - Real-world applications
- **Scholarly presentation** - Professional academic writing

### 4. Innovation Balance

- **Novel approaches** - New methods for studying phenomena
- **Established frameworks** - Grounding in accepted research
- **Technological integration** - Modern measurement techniques
- **Traditional wisdom** - Respect for historical knowledge

-----

## Potential Challenges and Solutions

### Challenge 1: Skeptical Reception

**Solution:** Emphasize methodological rigor and empirical evidence over interpretation

### Challenge 2: Ethical Concerns

**Solution:** Robust ethics review and participant protection protocols

### Challenge 3: Replication Difficulties

**Solution:** Detailed protocols and public data sharing where appropriate

### Challenge 4: Journal Bias

**Solution:** Target journals with history of publishing consciousness research

-----

- **Application Portal:** https://prms.cdsco.gov.in/
- **Contact:** ethics.cdsco@gov.in

- **Contact:** ethics@aiims.ac.in

## Part 2: Ethics Application Documentation Requirements

### 2.1 Required Forms and Documents

#### Standard Application Package

1. **IRB Application Form** (Institution-specific)
2. **Research Protocol** (Detailed methodology)
3. **Informed Consent Forms** (Participant and witness versions)
4. **Investigator Qualifications** (CV and training certificates)
5. **Risk Assessment** (Potential harms and mitigation strategies)
6. **Data Management Plan** (Storage, anonymization, destruction)
7. **Institutional Support Letter** (From True Religion Mission)

#### Additional Documents for Your Research

1. **Cultural Sensitivity Protocol** (Religious experience handling)
2. **Vulnerable Population Protection** (Emotional/psychological safeguards)
3. **Media/Recording Consent** (Photo/video permissions)
4. **Translator/Interpreter Agreements** (Multi-language considerations)
5. **Emergency Response Plan** (Psychological distress protocols)

### 2.2 Sample Application Timeline

- **Application Submission:** 4-6 weeks to prepare
- **Initial Review:** 2-4 weeks
- **Committee Meeting:** Monthly meetings (check schedules)
- **Approval/Revisions:** 2-8 weeks additional
- **Total Timeline:** 3-6 months

## Conclusion

These resources provide comprehensive support for your immediate next steps. The ethics review board application should be your absolute priority, as it has the longest timeline and is required before any participant recruitment can begin. Simultaneously, the literature review verification will strengthen your manuscript’s academic foundation.

**Primary Recommendation:** Begin with ICMR Ethics Committee application while setting up your literature review verification system using Zotero and PubMed access.

**Timeline:** Allow 4-6 months for ethics approval and 2-3 months for complete literature review verification.

**Success Metrics:**

- Ethics approval obtained
- Literature review updated with 2024-2025 sources
- Reference management system operational
- Ready to begin data collection phase

I’ve created comprehensive resources for your immediate next actions. Here are the key links and contacts you’ll need:

**Ethics Review Board Options:**

**Primary Recommendation - ICMR (Indian Council of Medical Research):**

- Website: https://www.icmr.gov.in/
- Ethics Guidelines: https://www.icmr.gov.in/guidelines.html
- Email: ethics@icmr.gov.in
- Phone: +91-11-26588980

**Alternative Options:**

- AIIMS New Delhi: https://www.aiims.edu/en/about-aiims/ethics-committee.html
- PGIMER Chandigarh: https://www.pgimer.edu.in/PGIMER_PORTAL/PGIMERPORTAL/home.jsp
- Central Ethics Committee: https://cdsco.gov.in/opencms/opencms/en/Approval/

**Literature Review Verification Resources:**

**Free Databases:**

**Immediate Timeline:**
